Hmm. As a huge Agatha Christie fan and as someone who was pleased enough with MOTOE to buy it on 4K Blu-Ray, I've been waiting for this trailer. And now that it's here . . . hmm . . . something feels off. This is a classic story set in the 1930s but this trailer does not feel particularly classic. I think they're trying too hard to make it feel modern and appeal to younger audiences. It's too sleek and sexed up, and lacks the quaint charm of Christie's story. My hope here is that it's just the TRAILER that feels this way and the movie will be different. The film will have to be good to give the '78 version a run for its money.
